Input
{
  "content": "# Migration Guide: Envoy External Processing Filter (ext_proc) v1.30 \u2192 v1.31\n\n## Overview\n\nEnvoy v1.31.0 (July 2024) delivers several targeted improvements to the External Processing (ext_proc) HTTP filter. The primary themes of this release are:\n\n- **Route cache control refinement**: A new `route_cache_action` enum field supersedes the binary `disable_clear_route_cache` flag, giving operators three-way control (default, always-clear, always-retain).\n- **Observability mode hardening**: The `observability_mode` feature (introduced in v1.30) gains an explicit `deferred_close_timeout` to prevent resource leaks from long-lived gRPC streams.\n- **Internal stream lifecycle change**: The gRPC stream is now managed by a thread-local `ThreadLocalStreamManager`, enabling the stream to outlive the filter instance in observability mode.\n\nThere are **no breaking changes** that require immediate configuration edits for operators not using `disable_clear_route_cache`. However, `disable_clear_route_cache` is marked for future deprecation and should be migrated to `route_cache_action`.\n\n---\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\n### 1. Mutual Exclusion of `disable_clear_route_cache` and `route_cache_action`\n\n**Status:** Runtime error (configuration rejected at startup)\n\nIn v1.31, if you set `disable_clear_route_cache: true` **and** a non-`DEFAULT` value for `route_cache_action` simultaneously, Envoy will throw an exception and refuse to start:\n\n```\ndisable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action can not be set to none-default at the same time.\n```\n\nOnly one of these two fields may be active at a time.\n\n**Source:** `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` (FilterConfig constructor)\n\n**Action required:** If your configuration sets both fields (e.g., from composing templates), remove one of them before upgrading.\n\n**Before (broken in v1.31 if both are non-default):**\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc_server\n      disable_clear_route_cache: true\n      route_cache_action: CLEAR   # ERROR: conflicts with disable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n**After (valid in v1.31):**\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc_server\n      route_cache_action: RETAIN   # Equivalent to disable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n---\n\n## Deprecated Features\n\n### 1. `disable_clear_route_cache` (field 11)\n\n**Proto:** `ExternalProcessor.disable_clear_route_cache` (`bool`, field 11)\n\n**Status:** Soft-deprecated in v1.31 via `udpa.annotations.field_migrate` annotation. The field continues to work in v1.31 but is scheduled for promotion into a `oneof` in a future release.\n\n**What changed:** The field now carries a `(udpa.annotations.field_migrate).oneof_promotion = \"clear_route_cache_type\"` annotation in `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto`. When `disable_clear_route_cache: true` is set and no `route_cache_action` is specified, the runtime silently maps it to `RouteCacheAction::RETAIN`.\n\n**Migration advice:** Replace `disable_clear_route_cache` with the equivalent `route_cache_action` value. The new field is more expressive and the old field will eventually be removed.\n\n| Old configuration | New equivalent |\n|---|---|\n| `disable_clear_route_cache: false` (or unset) | `route_cache_action: DEFAULT` (or unset) |\n| `disable_clear_route_cache: true` | `route_cache_action: RETAIN` |\n\n**Before (v1.30):**\n```yaml\ngrpc_service:\n  envoy_grpc:\n    cluster_name: ext_proc_server\ndisable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n**After (v1.31 recommended):**\n```yaml\ngrpc_service:\n  envoy_grpc:\n    cluster_name: ext_proc_server\nroute_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### 1. `RouteCacheAction` Enum and `route_cache_action` Field\n\n**Proto:** `ExternalProcessor.RouteCacheAction` (enum), `ExternalProcessor.route_cache_action` (field 18)\n\n**Source:** `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto`\n\nThis new enum provides three-way control over how Envoy handles its route cache when the external processor responds to request headers:\n\n| Value | Behavior |\n|---|---|\n| `DEFAULT` (0) | Clear route cache only when the `clear_route_cache` bit is set in the processor's `CommonResponse`. This was the pre-v1.30 behavior and remains the default. |\n| `CLEAR` (1) | Always clear the route cache unconditionally upon receiving a processor response for request headers, regardless of the `clear_route_cache` bit. |\n| `RETAIN` (2) | Never clear the route cache, ignoring the `clear_route_cache` bit entirely. Equivalent to the old `disable_clear_route_cache: true`. |\n\n**Use cases:**\n- Use `CLEAR` when your processor always modifies routing-significant headers (e.g., `:authority`, `x-forwarded-host`) and you want to guarantee route recomputation without depending on the processor to set the bit.\n- Use `RETAIN` when route cache invalidation is never needed, or when running in a read-only observability mode.\n- Leave as `DEFAULT` if you rely on the processor to signal cache invalidation case-by-case via `clear_route_cache`.\n\n**Example \u2014 always clear route cache:**\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc_server\n      processing_mode:\n        request_header_mode: SEND\n        response_header_mode: SEND\n      route_cache_action: CLEAR\n```\n\n---\n\n### 2. `deferred_close_timeout` Field for Observability Mode\n\n**Proto:** `ExternalProcessor.deferred_close_timeout` (`google.protobuf.Duration`, field 19)\n\n**Source:** `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto`, `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h`\n\n**Default:** 5000 milliseconds (5 seconds)\n\nWhen `observability_mode: true` is configured, the ext_proc gRPC stream may remain open to the external processor after the client-to-upstream HTTP stream has already completed (so the processor can finish consuming any buffered data). This new field sets the maximum duration Envoy will wait before forcibly closing that lingering gRPC stream.\n\nWithout this timeout, a slow or unresponsive processor could hold open gRPC streams indefinitely, leading to resource exhaustion.\n\n**Implementation detail:** Internally, v1.31 introduces a `ThreadLocalStreamManager` and `DeferredDeletableStream` class hierarchy (`source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h`) that holds the gRPC stream past the filter's `onDestroy()` call and fires a timer to close it after `deferred_close_timeout` elapses.\n\n**Example:**\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc_server\n      observability_mode: true\n      deferred_close_timeout:\n        seconds: 2       # Close lingering streams after 2 seconds (default is 5)\n```\n\n**Note:** `deferred_close_timeout` has no effect when `observability_mode: false`.\n\n---\n\n### 3. Observability Mode: `encodeComplete()` Hook and Stream Logging\n\n**Source:** `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h` (`Filter::encodeComplete()`), `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc`\n\nIn v1.31, when `observability_mode` is enabled the filter overrides `encodeComplete()` to call `logGrpcStreamInfo()` when the response encoding phase finishes. This ensures that gRPC call statistics (latency, bytes sent/received, cluster info, upstream host) are recorded to the filter state even when stream closure is deferred.\n\nThis is a behavioral enhancement rather than a configuration change, but operators monitoring `ExtProcLoggingInfo` filter-state data should be aware that in observability mode, logging now occurs at `encodeComplete` rather than at stream close.\n\n---\n\n### 4. `observability_mode` Flag Propagated on `ProcessingRequest`\n\n**Proto:** `ProcessingRequest.observability_mode` (`bool`, field 10 \u2014 in the service-side proto `api/envoy/service/ext_proc/v3/external_processor.proto`)\n\n**Source:** `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` (`buildHeaderRequest()`, `sendTrailers()`)\n\nIn v1.31, when the filter is running in observability mode, each `ProcessingRequest` message sent to the external processor now explicitly sets `observability_mode: true`. External processors can use this flag to know they must not send back a `ProcessingResponse` (since responses are ignored in this mode).\n\nExternal processor implementations that inspect `ProcessingRequest` should handle this flag gracefully \u2014 no response is expected or processed.\n\n---\n\n## Configuration Updates\n\n### Summary of Proto Field Changes\n\n| Field | v1.30 | v1.31 | Action |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `disable_clear_route_cache` (field 11) | `bool` | `bool` + deprecation annotation | Migrate to `route_cache_action: RETAIN` |\n| `route_cache_action` (field 18) | Not present | New `RouteCacheAction` enum field | Use instead of `disable_clear_route_cache` |\n| `deferred_close_timeout` (field 19) | Not present | New `Duration` field | Set when using `observability_mode: true` |\n| `RouteCacheAction` enum | Not present | New nested enum (`DEFAULT`, `CLEAR`, `RETAIN`) | Use with `route_cache_action` |\n\n### Recommended v1.31 Configuration Template\n\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n\n      # Required: gRPC service endpoint\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc_server\n\n      # Processing mode (unchanged from v1.30)\n      processing_mode:\n        request_header_mode: SEND\n        response_header_mode: SEND\n        request_body_mode: NONE\n        response_body_mode: NONE\n\n      # UPDATED: use route_cache_action instead of disable_clear_route_cache\n      # Options: DEFAULT (default), CLEAR, RETAIN\n      route_cache_action: DEFAULT\n\n      # Timeouts (unchanged from v1.30)\n      message_timeout:\n        nanos: 200000000    # 200ms default\n      max_message_timeout:\n        seconds: 10\n\n      # Observability mode (v1.30+), now with deferred_close_timeout (v1.31+)\n      # observability_mode: true\n      # deferred_close_timeout:\n      #   seconds: 5        # Default is 5 seconds\n\n      # Other settings (unchanged)\n      failure_mode_allow: false\n      allow_mode_override: false\n```\n\n---\n\n## Migration Steps\n\n### Step 1: Audit `disable_clear_route_cache` Usage\n\nSearch your Envoy configurations for any use of `disable_clear_route_cache`:\n\n```bash\ngrep -r \"disable_clear_route_cache\" /path/to/envoy/configs/\n```\n\nFor each occurrence:\n- If `disable_clear_route_cache: true` \u2192 replace with `route_cache_action: RETAIN`\n- If `disable_clear_route_cache: false` \u2192 remove the field (it is the default behavior)\n\n### Step 2: Check for Conflicting Configuration\n\nEnsure no configuration sets both `disable_clear_route_cache` (non-false) and `route_cache_action` (non-DEFAULT) at the same time. This will cause Envoy to fail to start in v1.31.\n\n```bash\n# Identify any files that have both fields\ngrep -l \"disable_clear_route_cache\" /path/to/configs/ | xargs grep -l \"route_cache_action\"\n```\n\n### Step 3: Configure `deferred_close_timeout` for Observability Mode\n\nIf you use `observability_mode: true`, add an explicit `deferred_close_timeout` appropriate for your processor's expected response latency. The default (5 seconds) is conservative:\n\n```yaml\nobservability_mode: true\ndeferred_close_timeout:\n  seconds: 2   # Tune based on your processor's observed drain time\n```\n\n### Step 4: Validate Processor Behavior in Observability Mode\n\nIf using observability mode, update your external processor implementation to:\n1. Check for `observability_mode: true` on each `ProcessingRequest`.\n2. Skip sending a `ProcessingResponse` when observability mode is active.\n3. Expect the gRPC stream to be closed by Envoy after `deferred_close_timeout` elapses, not immediately at request completion.\n\n### Step 5: Update Any `FilterConfig` C++ Code (if embedding Envoy)\n\nIf you build Envoy as a library and directly instantiate `FilterConfig`:\n\n- The `disableClearRouteCache()` method is removed. Use `routeCacheAction()` which returns `ExternalProcessor::RouteCacheAction`.\n- The `FilterConfig` constructor now accepts the full proto config and internally reads `observability_mode` and `deferred_close_timeout`.\n- `FilterConfig::threadLocalStreamManager()` is a new method for accessing the per-thread stream manager; do not manage gRPC stream lifetimes directly.\n\n### Step 6: Rebuild and Test in a Staging Environment\n\nDeploy the v1.31 binary to a staging environment with your updated configuration and run integration tests before promoting to production.\n\n---\n\n## Testing Recommendations\n\n### Configuration Validation\n\n1. **Start Envoy with the updated config** and check for startup errors. A conflict between `disable_clear_route_cache` and `route_cache_action` will surface immediately as a logged exception.\n\n2. **Verify route cache behavior** by sending requests through routes that require header-based routing decisions after ext_proc mutation:\n   - With `route_cache_action: DEFAULT`: Confirm the processor's `clear_route_cache` bit correctly triggers route recomputation.\n   - With `route_cache_action: CLEAR`: Confirm that the route is always recomputed after a processor response, even without the bit.\n   - With `route_cache_action: RETAIN`: Confirm that header changes from the processor do not alter the selected route.\n\n3. **Observability mode timeout**: If testing `observability_mode`, inject artificial latency into your processor and confirm that Envoy closes the gRPC stream after `deferred_close_timeout` without blocking request processing.\n\n### Statistics to Monitor\n\nAll statistics from v1.30 are retained. Key counters relevant to the migrated features:\n\n| Stat | Meaning |\n|---|---|\n| `ext_proc.clear_route_cache_ignored` | Route cache clear was requested but ignored (e.g., under `RETAIN`) |\n| `ext_proc.clear_route_cache_disabled` | Route cache clear was rejected because it was disabled |\n| `ext_proc.streams_closed` | gRPC streams cleanly closed (includes deferred closes in observability mode) |\n| `ext_proc.streams_failed` | gRPC stream errors \u2014 watch for spikes after migration |\n\nMonitor `clear_route_cache_ignored` and `clear_route_cache_disabled` before and after switching from `disable_clear_route_cache` to `route_cache_action: RETAIN` to confirm equivalent behavior.\n\n### Integration Tests\n\nRun the existing ext_proc integration test suite against the v1.31 binary:\n\n```\ntest/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc_integration_test.cc\ntest/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/filter_test.cc\n```\n\nIn particular, the following test cases exercise the new features:\n- `ObservabilityModeWithFullRequest` \u2014 deferred close with full request body\n- `ObservabilityModeWithFullResponse` \u2014 deferred close with full response body\n- `ObservabilityModeWithLoggingCloseStream` \u2014 stream logging at `encodeComplete`\n- Tests around `route_cache_action: CLEAR` and combined `disable_clear_route_cache` + `route_cache_action` conflict detection\n\n---\n\n## Rollback Guidance\n\nIf you need to roll back from v1.31 to v1.30:\n\n1. **`route_cache_action` field**: v1.30 does not recognize this field. If your control plane uses xDS-based configuration, ensure the xDS server does not push `route_cache_action` to v1.30 proxies \u2014 unknown proto3 fields are silently ignored, but the intended behavior (CLEAR/RETAIN) will be lost.\n\n   **Risk**: If you replaced `disable_clear_route_cache: true` with `route_cache_action: RETAIN` and roll back to v1.30, the `route_cache_action` field will be silently ignored and route cache clearing will resume (revert to `DEFAULT` behavior). If this is undesirable, restore `disable_clear_route_cache: true` before rolling back.\n\n2. **`deferred_close_timeout` field**: v1.30 does not recognize this field. It will be silently ignored on rollback with no functional impact (v1.30 does not support deferred stream closure at all \u2014 the stream is closed synchronously).\n\n3. **Observability mode stream lifecycle**: v1.30 uses a `unique_ptr`-owned gRPC stream that is destroyed with the filter. Processor implementations expecting the deferred-close behavior of v1.31 will instead see the stream closed immediately at request completion when running against v1.30.\n\n### Rollback Checklist\n\n- [ ] Restore `disable_clear_route_cache: true` on any configs that were migrated to `route_cache_action: RETAIN` (to preserve behavior under v1.30)\n- [ ] Remove `route_cache_action` from static configuration files sent to v1.30 proxies if behavior consistency is critical\n- [ ] Alert your processor team that `deferred_close_timeout` will no longer be honored and streams will close at request end\n- [ ] Revert the Envoy binary and restart with the original v1.30 configuration\n",

  "content": "# Migration Guide: Envoy External Processing Filter (ext_proc) v1.30 \u2192 v1.31\n\n## Overview\n\nEnvoy v1.31.0 (July 2024) delivers several targeted improvements to the External Processing (ext_proc) HTTP filter. The primary themes of this release are:\n\n- **Route cache control refinement**: A new `route_cache_action` enum field supersedes the binary `disable_clear_route_cache` flag, giving operators three-way control (default, always-clear, always-retain).\n- **Observability mode hardening**: The `observability_mode` feature (introduced in v1.30) gains an explicit `deferred_close_timeout` to prevent resource leaks from long-lived gRPC streams.\n- **Internal stream lifecycle change**: The gRPC stream is now managed by a thread-local `ThreadLocalStreamManager`, enabling the stream to outlive the filter instance in observability mode.\n\nThere are **no breaking changes** that require immediate configuration edits for operators not using `disable_clear_route_cache`. However, `disable_clear_route_cache` is marked for future deprecation and should be migrated to `route_cache_action`.\n\n---\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\n### 1. Mutual Exclusion of `disable_clear_route_cache` and `route_cache_action`\n\n**Status:** Runtime error (configuration rejected at startup)\n\nIn v1.31, if you set `disable_clear_route_cache: true` **and** a non-`DEFAULT` value for `route_cache_action` simultaneously, Envoy will throw an exception and refuse to start:\n\n```\ndisable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action can not be set to none-default at the same time.\n```\n\nOnly one of these two fields may be active at a time.\n\n**Source:** `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` (FilterConfig constructor)\n\n**Action required:** If your configuration sets both fields (e.g., from composing templates), remove one of them before upgrading.\n\n**Before (broken in v1.31 if both are non-default):**\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc_server\n      disable_clear_route_cache: true\n      route_cache_action: CLEAR   # ERROR: conflicts with disable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n**After (valid in v1.31):**\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc_server\n      route_cache_action: RETAIN   # Equivalent to disable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n---\n\n## Deprecated Features\n\n### 1. `disable_clear_route_cache` (field 11)\n\n**Proto:** `ExternalProcessor.disable_clear_route_cache` (`bool`, field 11)\n\n**Status:** Soft-deprecated in v1.31 via `udpa.annotations.field_migrate` annotation. The field continues to work in v1.31 but is scheduled for promotion into a `oneof` in a future release.\n\n**What changed:** The field now carries a `(udpa.annotations.field_migrate).oneof_promotion = \"clear_route_cache_type\"` annotation in `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto`. When `disable_clear_route_cache: true` is set and no `route_cache_action` is specified, the runtime silently maps it to `RouteCacheAction::RETAIN`.\n\n**Migration advice:** Replace `disable_clear_route_cache` with the equivalent `route_cache_action` value. The new field is more expressive and the old field will eventually be removed.\n\n| Old configuration | New equivalent |\n|---|---|\n| `disable_clear_route_cache: false` (or unset) | `route_cache_action: DEFAULT` (or unset) |\n| `disable_clear_route_cache: true` | `route_cache_action: RETAIN` |\n\n**Before (v1.30):**\n```yaml\ngrpc_service:\n  envoy_grpc:\n    cluster_name: ext_proc_server\ndisable_clear_route_cache: true\n```\n\n**After (v1.31 recommended):**\n```yaml\ngrpc_service:\n  envoy_grpc:\n    cluster_name: ext_proc_server\nroute_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### 1. `RouteCacheAction` Enum and `route_cache_action` Field\n\n**Proto:** `ExternalProcessor.RouteCacheAction` (enum), `ExternalProcessor.route_cache_action` (field 18)\n\n**Source:** `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto`\n\nThis new enum provides three-way control over how Envoy handles its route cache when the external processor responds to request headers:\n\n| Value | Behavior |\n|---|---|\n| `DEFAULT` (0) | Clear route cache only when the `clear_route_cache` bit is set in the processor's `CommonResponse`. This was the pre-v1.30 behavior and remains the default. |\n| `CLEAR` (1) | Always clear the route cache unconditionally upon receiving a processor response for request headers, regardless of the `clear_route_cache` bit. |\n| `RETAIN` (2) | Never clear the route cache, ignoring the `clear_route_cache` bit entirely. Equivalent to the old `disable_clear_route_cache: true`. |\n\n**Use cases:**\n- Use `CLEAR` when your processor always modifies routing-significant headers (e.g., `:authority`, `x-forwarded-host`) and you want to guarantee route recomputation without depending on the processor to set the bit.\n- Use `RETAIN` when route cache invalidation is never needed, or when running in a read-only observability mode.\n- Leave as `DEFAULT` if you rely on the processor to signal cache invalidation case-by-case via `clear_route_cache`.\n\n**Example \u2014 always clear route cache:**\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc_server\n      processing_mode:\n        request_header_mode: SEND\n        response_header_mode: SEND\n      route_cache_action: CLEAR\n```\n\n---\n\n### 2. `deferred_close_timeout` Field for Observability Mode\n\n**Proto:** `ExternalProcessor.deferred_close_timeout` (`google.protobuf.Duration`, field 19)\n\n**Source:** `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto`, `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h`\n\n**Default:** 5000 milliseconds (5 seconds)\n\nWhen `observability_mode: true` is configured, the ext_proc gRPC stream may remain open to the external processor after the client-to-upstream HTTP stream has already completed (so the processor can finish consuming any buffered data). This new field sets the maximum duration Envoy will wait before forcibly closing that lingering gRPC stream.\n\nWithout this timeout, a slow or unresponsive processor could hold open gRPC streams indefinitely, leading to resource exhaustion.\n\n**Implementation detail:** Internally, v1.31 introduces a `ThreadLocalStreamManager` and `DeferredDeletableStream` class hierarchy (`source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h`) that holds the gRPC stream past the filter's `onDestroy()` call and fires a timer to close it after `deferred_close_timeout` elapses.\n\n**Example:**\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc_server\n      observability_mode: true\n      deferred_close_timeout:\n        seconds: 2       # Close lingering streams after 2 seconds (default is 5)\n```\n\n**Note:** `deferred_close_timeout` has no effect when `observability_mode: false`.\n\n---\n\n### 3. Observability Mode: `encodeComplete()` Hook and Stream Logging\n\n**Source:** `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h` (`Filter::encodeComplete()`), `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc`\n\nIn v1.31, when `observability_mode` is enabled the filter overrides `encodeComplete()` to call `logGrpcStreamInfo()` when the response encoding phase finishes. This ensures that gRPC call statistics (latency, bytes sent/received, cluster info, upstream host) are recorded to the filter state even when stream closure is deferred.\n\nThis is a behavioral enhancement rather than a configuration change, but operators monitoring `ExtProcLoggingInfo` filter-state data should be aware that in observability mode, logging now occurs at `encodeComplete` rather than at stream close.\n\n---\n\n### 4. `observability_mode` Flag Propagated on `ProcessingRequest`\n\n**Proto:** `ProcessingRequest.observability_mode` (`bool`, field 10 \u2014 in the service-side proto `api/envoy/service/ext_proc/v3/external_processor.proto`)\n\n**Source:** `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` (`buildHeaderRequest()`, `sendTrailers()`)\n\nIn v1.31, when the filter is running in observability mode, each `ProcessingRequest` message sent to the external processor now explicitly sets `observability_mode: true`. External processors can use this flag to know they must not send back a `ProcessingResponse` (since responses are ignored in this mode).\n\nExternal processor implementations that inspect `ProcessingRequest` should handle this flag gracefully \u2014 no response is expected or processed.\n\n---\n\n## Configuration Updates\n\n### Summary of Proto Field Changes\n\n| Field | v1.30 | v1.31 | Action |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `disable_clear_route_cache` (field 11) | `bool` | `bool` + deprecation annotation | Migrate to `route_cache_action: RETAIN` |\n| `route_cache_action` (field 18) | Not present | New `RouteCacheAction` enum field | Use instead of `disable_clear_route_cache` |\n| `deferred_close_timeout` (field 19) | Not present | New `Duration` field | Set when using `observability_mode: true` |\n| `RouteCacheAction` enum | Not present | New nested enum (`DEFAULT`, `CLEAR`, `RETAIN`) | Use with `route_cache_action` |\n\n### Recommended v1.31 Configuration Template\n\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n\n      # Required: gRPC service endpoint\n      grpc_service:\n        envoy_grpc:\n          cluster_name: ext_proc_server\n\n      # Processing mode (unchanged from v1.30)\n      processing_mode:\n        request_header_mode: SEND\n        response_header_mode: SEND\n        request_body_mode: NONE\n        response_body_mode: NONE\n\n      # UPDATED: use route_cache_action instead of disable_clear_route_cache\n      # Options: DEFAULT (default), CLEAR, RETAIN\n      route_cache_action: DEFAULT\n\n      # Timeouts (unchanged from v1.30)\n      message_timeout:\n        nanos: 200000000    # 200ms default\n      max_message_timeout:\n        seconds: 10\n\n      # Observability mode (v1.30+), now with deferred_close_timeout (v1.31+)\n      # observability_mode: true\n      # deferred_close_timeout:\n      #   seconds: 5        # Default is 5 seconds\n\n      # Other settings (unchanged)\n      failure_mode_allow: false\n      allow_mode_override: false\n```\n\n---\n\n## Migration Steps\n\n### Step 1: Audit `disable_clear_route_cache` Usage\n\nSearch your Envoy configurations for any use of `disable_clear_route_cache`:\n\n```bash\ngrep -r \"disable_clear_route_cache\" /path/to/envoy/configs/\n```\n\nFor each occurrence:\n- If `disable_clear_route_cache: true` \u2192 replace with `route_cache_action: RETAIN`\n- If `disable_clear_route_cache: false` \u2192 remove the field (it is the default behavior)\n\n### Step 2: Check for Conflicting Configuration\n\nEnsure no configuration sets both `disable_clear_route_cache` (non-false) and `route_cache_action` (non-DEFAULT) at the same time.         Code Changes (1)
        
1. WRITE /workspace/documentation.md
# Migration Guide: Envoy External Processing Filter (ext_proc) v1.30 → v1.31

## Overview

Envoy v1.31.0 (July 2024) delivers several targeted improvements to the External Processing (ext_proc) HTTP filter. The primary themes of this release are:

- **Route cache control refinement**: A new `route_cache_action` enum field supersedes the binary `disable_clear_route_cache` flag, giving operators three-way control (default, always-clear, always-retain).
- **Observability mode hardening**: The `observability_mode` feature (introduced in v1.30) gains an explicit `deferred_close_timeout` to prevent resource leaks from long-lived gRPC streams.
- **Internal stream lifecycle change**: The gRPC stream is now managed by a thread-local `ThreadLocalStreamManager`, enabling the stream to outlive the filter instance in observability mode.

There are **no breaking changes** that require immediate configuration edits for operators not using `disable_clear_route_cache`. However, `disable_clear_route_cache` is marked for future deprecation and should be migrated to `route_cache_action`.

---

## Breaking Changes

### 1. Mutual Exclusion of `disable_clear_route_cache` and `route_cache_action`

**Status:** Runtime error (configuration rejected at startup)

In v1.31, if you set `disable_clear_route_cache: true` **and** a non-`DEFAULT` value for `route_cache_action` simultaneously, Envoy will throw an exception and refuse to start:

```
disable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action can not be set to none-default at the same time.
```

Only one of these two fields may be active at a time.

**Source:** `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` (FilterConfig constructor)
